</div>
			<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">List of colleges and universities in the United States by endowment</h1>
									<div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content">
									<div id="siteSub" class="noprint">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
								<div id="contentSub"></div>
												<div id="jump-to-nav" class="mw-jump">
					Jump to:					<a href="#mw-head">navigation</a>, 					<a href="#p-search">search</a>
				</div>
				<div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="mw-parser-output"><div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Harvard_college_-_annenberg_hall.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d3/Harvard_college_-_annenberg_hall.jpg/220px-Harvard_college_-_annenberg_hall.jpg" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d3/Harvard_college_-_annenberg_hall.jpg/330px-Harvard_college_-_annenberg_hall.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d3/Harvard_college_-_annenberg_hall.jpg/440px-Harvard_college_-_annenberg_hall.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1024" data-file-height="768" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Harvard_college_-_annenberg_hall.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Annenberg Hall at <a href="/wiki/Harvard_University" title="Harvard University">Harvard University</a>, which has the largest endowment in the United States</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>This following is a <b>list of U.S. institutions of higher education with <a href="/wiki/Financial_endowment" title="Financial endowment">endowments</a></b> greater than one billion dollars according to National Association of College and University Business Officers (NACUBO).<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup></p>
<p>Since colleges and universities vary greatly in terms of the size of their student bodies, a table with endowment per student figures is included as well. For example, <a href="/wiki/Princeton_University" title="Princeton University">Princeton University</a>'s endowment is smaller than <a href="/wiki/Harvard_University" title="Harvard University">Harvard University</a>'s, yet <a href="/wiki/Princeton_University" title="Princeton University">Princeton University</a>'s endowment per student figure is larger than <a href="/wiki/Harvard_University" title="Harvard University">Harvard University</a>'s at $2.8 million per student.</p>
<p>In 2005,the endowment table below totaled $219.37 Billion. At the end of 2015 the table totals $394.96 Billion, an increase of 80% in billion dollar university endowments.</p>
<p></p>
